<h1 class="class" style="margin-bottom: 0.75em; font-size: 2em; line-height: 1.5; font-family: Georgia, 'Times New Roman', serif; color: rgb(108, 108, 108);">Net::HTTP</h1><div id="description" class="description" style="font-size: 16px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: Georgia, 'Times New Roman', serif; line-height: 24px;"><h2 id="class-Net::HTTP-label-An+HTTP+client+API+for+Ruby." style="margin-bottom: 1em; font-size: 1.5em; line-height: 1; font-family: Georgia, 'Times New Roman', serif; color: rgb(108, 108, 108);">An&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: none; color: rgb(204, 51, 51);">HTTP</a>&nbsp;client API for Ruby.<span style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#class-Net::HTTP-label-An+HTTP+client+API+for+Ruby." style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: none; color: rgb(204, 51, 51);">¶</a>&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#top" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: none; color: rgb(204, 51, 51);">↑&lt;/a></span></h2><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP</a>&nbsp;provides a rich library which can be used to build&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTP</a>&nbsp;user-agents. For more details about&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTP</a>&nbsp;see [RFC2616](<a href="http://www.ietf.org/rfc/rfc2616.txt" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">www.ietf.org/rfc/rfc2616.txt</a>)</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP</a>&nbsp;is designed to work closely with URI. URI::HTTP#host, URI::HTTP#port and URI::HTTP#request_uri are designed to work with<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP</a>.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;">If you are only performing a few GET requests you should try OpenURI.</p><h2 id="class-Net::HTTP-label-Simple+Examples" style="margin-bottom: 1em; font-size: 1.5em; line-height: 1; font-family: Georgia, 'Times New Roman', serif; color: rgb(108, 108, 108);">Simple Examples<span style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#class-Net::HTTP-label-Simple+Examples" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: none; color: rgb(204, 51, 51);">¶</a>&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#top" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: none; color: rgb(204, 51, 51);">↑&lt;/a></span></h2><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;">All examples assume you have loaded&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP</a>&nbsp;with:</p><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(48, 48, 48);"><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">require</span> <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'net/http'</span>
</pre><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;">This will also require ‘uri’ so you don’t need to require it separately.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;">The&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP</a>&nbsp;methods in the following section do not persist connections. They are not recommended if you are performing many&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTP</a>&nbsp;requests.</p><h3 id="class-Net::HTTP-label-GET" style="margin-bottom: 1.2em; font-size: 1.25em; line-height: 1.2; font-family: Georgia, 'Times New Roman', serif; color: rgb(108, 108, 108);">GET<span style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#class-Net::HTTP-label-GET" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">¶</a>&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#top" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">↑&lt;/a></span></h3><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(48, 48, 48);"><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTP</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">get</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'example.com'</span>, <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'/index.html'</span>) <span class="ruby-comment" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(94, 255, 31); font-weight: bold; background: transparent;"># =&gt; String</span>
</pre><h3 id="class-Net::HTTP-label-GET+by+URI" style="margin-bottom: 1.2em; font-size: 1.25em; line-height: 1.2; font-family: Georgia, 'Times New Roman', serif; color: rgb(108, 108, 108);">GET by URI<span style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#class-Net::HTTP-label-GET+by+URI" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">¶</a>&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#top" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">↑&lt;/a></span></h3><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(48, 48, 48);"><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">URI</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'http://example.com/index.html?count=10'</span>)
<span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTP</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">get</span>(<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span>) <span class="ruby-comment" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(94, 255, 31); font-weight: bold; background: transparent;"># =&gt; String</span>
</pre><h3 id="class-Net::HTTP-label-GET+with+Dynamic+Parameters" style="margin-bottom: 1.2em; font-size: 1.25em; line-height: 1.2; font-family: Georgia, 'Times New Roman', serif; color: rgb(108, 108, 108);">GET with Dynamic Parameters<span style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#class-Net::HTTP-label-GET+with+Dynamic+Parameters" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">¶</a>&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#top" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">↑&lt;/a></span></h3><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(48, 48, 48);"><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">URI</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'http://example.com/index.html'</span>)
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">params</span> = { :<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">limit</span> =<span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">&gt;</span> <span class="ruby-value" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">10</span>, :<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">page</span> =<span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">&gt;</span> <span class="ruby-value" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">3</span> }
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">query</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">URI</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">encode_www_form</span>(<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">params</span>)

<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">res</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTP</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">get_response</span>(<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span>)
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">puts</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">res</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">body</span> <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">if</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">res</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">is_a?</span>(<span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTPSuccess</span>)
</pre><h3 id="class-Net::HTTP-label-POST" style="margin-bottom: 1.2em; font-size: 1.25em; line-height: 1.2; font-family: Georgia, 'Times New Roman', serif; color: rgb(108, 108, 108);">POST<span style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#class-Net::HTTP-label-POST" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">¶</a>&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#top" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">↑&lt;/a></span></h3><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(48, 48, 48);"><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">URI</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'http://www.example.com/search.cgi'</span>)
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">res</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTP</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">post_form</span>(<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span>, <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'q'</span> =<span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">&gt;</span> <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'ruby'</span>, <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'max'</span> =<span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">&gt;</span> <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'50'</span>)
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">puts</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">res</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">body</span>
</pre><h3 id="class-Net::HTTP-label-POST+with+Multiple+Values" style="margin-bottom: 1.2em; font-size: 1.25em; line-height: 1.2; font-family: Georgia, 'Times New Roman', serif; color: rgb(108, 108, 108);">POST with Multiple Values<span style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#class-Net::HTTP-label-POST+with+Multiple+Values" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">¶</a>&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#top" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">↑&lt;/a></span></h3><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(48, 48, 48);"><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">URI</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'http://www.example.com/search.cgi'</span>)
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">res</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTP</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">post_form</span>(<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span>, <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'q'</span> =<span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">&gt;</span> [<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'ruby'</span>, <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'perl'</span>], <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'max'</span> =<span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">&gt;</span> <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'50'</span>)
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">puts</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">res</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">body</span>
</pre><h2 id="class-Net::HTTP-label-How+to+use+Net-3A-3AHTTP" style="margin-bottom: 1em; font-size: 1.5em; line-height: 1; font-family: Georgia, 'Times New Roman', serif; color: rgb(108, 108, 108);">How to use&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: none; color: rgb(204, 51, 51);">Net::HTTP</a><span style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#class-Net::HTTP-label-How+to+use+Net-3A-3AHTTP" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: none; color: rgb(204, 51, 51);">¶</a>&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#top" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: none; color: rgb(204, 51, 51);">↑&lt;/a></span></h2><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;">The following example code can be used as the basis of a&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTP</a>&nbsp;user-agent which can perform a variety of request types using persistent connections.</p><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(48, 48, 48);"><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">URI</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'http://example.com/some_path?query=string'</span>)

<span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTP</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">start</span>(<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">host</span>, <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">port</span>) <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">do</span> <span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">http</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span>
  <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">request</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTP</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Get</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">new</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span>

  <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">response</span> = <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">http</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">request</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">request</span> <span class="ruby-comment" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(94, 255, 31); font-weight: bold; background: transparent;"># Net::HTTPResponse object</span>
<span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">end</span>
</pre><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#method-c-start" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">::start</a>&nbsp;immediately creates a connection to an&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTP</a>&nbsp;server which is kept open for the duration of the block. The connection will remain open for multiple requests in the block if the server indicates it supports persistent connections.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;">The request types&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP</a>&nbsp;supports are listed below in the section “HTTP Request Classes”.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;">If you wish to re-use a connection across multiple&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTP</a>&nbsp;requests without automatically closing it you can use&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#method-c-new" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">::new</a>&nbsp;instead of&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#method-c-start" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">::start</a>.&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#method-i-request" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">request</a>&nbsp;will automatically open a connection to the server if one is not currently open. You can manually close the connection with&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#method-i-finish" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">finish</a>.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;">For all the&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP</a>&nbsp;request objects and shortcut request methods you may supply either a String for the request path or a URI from which&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP</a>will extract the request path.</p><h3 id="class-Net::HTTP-label-Response+Data" style="margin-bottom: 1.2em; font-size: 1.25em; line-height: 1.2; font-family: Georgia, 'Times New Roman', serif; color: rgb(108, 108, 108);">Response Data<span style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#class-Net::HTTP-label-Response+Data" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">¶</a>&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#top" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">↑&lt;/a></span></h3><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(48, 48, 48);"><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">URI</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'http://example.com/index.html'</span>)
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">res</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTP</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">get_response</span>(<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span>)

<span class="ruby-comment" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(94, 255, 31); font-weight: bold; background: transparent;"># Headers</span>
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">res</span>[<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'Set-Cookie'</span>]            <span class="ruby-comment" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(94, 255, 31); font-weight: bold; background: transparent;"># =&gt; String</span>
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">res</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">get_fields</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'set-cookie'</span>) <span class="ruby-comment" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(94, 255, 31); font-weight: bold; background: transparent;"># =&gt; Array</span>
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">res</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">to_hash</span>[<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'set-cookie'</span>]    <span class="ruby-comment" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(94, 255, 31); font-weight: bold; background: transparent;"># =&gt; Array</span>
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">puts</span> <span class="ruby-node" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 160, 122); background: transparent;">"Headers: #{res.to_hash.inspect}"</span>

<span class="ruby-comment" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(94, 255, 31); font-weight: bold; background: transparent;"># Status</span>
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">puts</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">res</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">code</span>       <span class="ruby-comment" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(94, 255, 31); font-weight: bold; background: transparent;"># =&gt; '200'</span>
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">puts</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">res</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">message</span>    <span class="ruby-comment" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(94, 255, 31); font-weight: bold; background: transparent;"># =&gt; 'OK'</span>
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">puts</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">res</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">class</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">name</span> <span class="ruby-comment" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(94, 255, 31); font-weight: bold; background: transparent;"># =&gt; 'HTTPOK'</span>

<span class="ruby-comment" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(94, 255, 31); font-weight: bold; background: transparent;"># Body</span>
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">puts</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">res</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">body</span> <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">if</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">res</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">response_body_permitted?</span>
</pre><h3 id="class-Net::HTTP-label-Following+Redirection" style="margin-bottom: 1.2em; font-size: 1.25em; line-height: 1.2; font-family: Georgia, 'Times New Roman', serif; color: rgb(108, 108, 108);">Following Redirection<span style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#class-Net::HTTP-label-Following+Redirection" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">¶</a>&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#top" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">↑&lt;/a></span></h3><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;">Each&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTPResponse.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTPResponse</a>&nbsp;object belongs to a class for its response code.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;">For example, all 2XX responses are instances of a&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTPSuccess.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTPSuccess</a>subclass, a 3XX response is an instance of a&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTPRedirection.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTPRedirection</a>&nbsp;subclass and a 200 response is an instance of the&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTPOK.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTPOK</a>&nbsp;class. For details of response classes, see the section “HTTP Response Classes” below.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;">Using a case statement you can handle various types of responses properly:</p><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(48, 48, 48);"><span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">def</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">fetch</span>(<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri_str</span>, <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">limit</span> = <span class="ruby-value" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">10</span>)
  <span class="ruby-comment" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(94, 255, 31); font-weight: bold; background: transparent;"># You should choose a better exception.</span>
  <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">raise</span> <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">ArgumentError</span>, <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'too many HTTP redirects'</span> <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">if</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">limit</span> <span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">==</span> <span class="ruby-value" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">0</span>

  <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">response</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTP</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">get_response</span>(<span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">URI</span>(<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri_str</span>))

  <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">case</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">response</span>
  <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">when</span> <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTPSuccess</span> <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">then</span>
    <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">response</span>
  <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">when</span> <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTPRedirection</span> <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">then</span>
    <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">location</span> = <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">response</span>[<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'location'</span>]
    <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">warn</span> <span class="ruby-node" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 160, 122); background: transparent;">"redirected to #{location}"</span>
    <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">fetch</span>(<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">location</span>, <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">limit</span> <span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">-</span> <span class="ruby-value" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">1</span>)
  <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">else</span>
    <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">response</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">value</span>
  <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">end</span>
<span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">end</span>

<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">print</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">fetch</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'http://www.ruby-lang.org'</span>)
</pre><h3 id="class-Net::HTTP-label-POST" style="margin-bottom: 1.2em; font-size: 1.25em; line-height: 1.2; font-family: Georgia, 'Times New Roman', serif; color: rgb(108, 108, 108);">POST<span style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#class-Net::HTTP-label-POST" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">¶</a>&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#top" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">↑&lt;/a></span></h3><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;">A POST can be made using the&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP/Post.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP::Post</a>&nbsp;request class. This example creates a urlencoded POST body:</p><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(48, 48, 48);"><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">URI</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'http://www.example.com/todo.cgi'</span>)
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">req</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTP</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Post</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">new</span>(<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span>)
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">req</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">set_form_data</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'from'</span> =<span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">&gt;</span> <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'2005-01-01'</span>, <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'to'</span> =<span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">&gt;</span> <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'2005-03-31'</span>)

<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">res</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTP</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">start</span>(<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">hostname</span>, <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">port</span>) <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">do</span> <span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">http</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span>
  <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">http</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">request</span>(<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">req</span>)
<span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">end</span>

<span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">case</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">res</span>
<span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">when</span> <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTPSuccess</span>, <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTPRedirection</span>
  <span class="ruby-comment" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(94, 255, 31); font-weight: bold; background: transparent;"># OK</span>
<span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">else</span>
  <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">res</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">value</span>
<span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">end</span>
</pre><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;">At this time&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP</a>&nbsp;does not support multipart/form-data. To send multipart/form-data use&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTPGenericRequest.html#method-i-body-3D" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTPGenericRequest#body=</a>&nbsp;and<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTPHeader.html#method-i-content_type-3D" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTPHeader#content_type=</a>:</p><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(48, 48, 48);"><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">req</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTP</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Post</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">new</span>(<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span>)
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">req</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">body</span> = <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">multipart_data</span>
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">req</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">content_type</span> = <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'multipart/form-data'</span>
</pre><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;">Other requests that can contain a body such as PUT can be created in the same way using the corresponding request class (Net::HTTP::Put).</p><h3 id="class-Net::HTTP-label-Setting+Headers" style="margin-bottom: 1.2em; font-size: 1.25em; line-height: 1.2; font-family: Georgia, 'Times New Roman', serif; color: rgb(108, 108, 108);">Setting Headers<span style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#class-Net::HTTP-label-Setting+Headers" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">¶</a>&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#top" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">↑&lt;/a></span></h3><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;">The following example performs a conditional GET using the If-Modified-Since header. If the files has not been modified since the time in the header a Not Modified response will be returned. See RFC 2616 section 9.3 for further details.</p><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(48, 48, 48);"><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">URI</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'http://example.com/cached_response'</span>)
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">file</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">File</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">stat</span> <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'cached_response'</span>

<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">req</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTP</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Get</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">new</span>(<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span>)
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">req</span>[<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'If-Modified-Since'</span>] = <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">file</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">mtime</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">rfc2822</span>

<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">res</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTP</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">start</span>(<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">hostname</span>, <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">port</span>) {<span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">http</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span>
  <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">http</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">request</span>(<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">req</span>)
}

<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">open</span> <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'cached_response'</span>, <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'w'</span> <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">do</span> <span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">io</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span>
  <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">io</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">write</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">res</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">body</span>
<span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">end</span> <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">if</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">res</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">is_a?</span>(<span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTPSuccess</span>)
</pre><h3 id="class-Net::HTTP-label-Basic+Authentication" style="margin-bottom: 1.2em; font-size: 1.25em; line-height: 1.2; font-family: Georgia, 'Times New Roman', serif; color: rgb(108, 108, 108);">Basic Authentication<span style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#class-Net::HTTP-label-Basic+Authentication" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">¶</a>&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#top" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">↑&lt;/a></span></h3><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;">Basic authentication is performed according to [RFC2617](<a href="http://www.ietf.org/rfc/rfc2617.txt" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">www.ietf.org/rfc/rfc2617.txt</a>)</p><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(48, 48, 48);"><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">URI</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'http://example.com/index.html?key=value'</span>)

<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">req</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTP</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Get</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">new</span>(<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span>)
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">req</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">basic_auth</span> <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'user'</span>, <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'pass'</span>

<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">res</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTP</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">start</span>(<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">hostname</span>, <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">port</span>) {<span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">http</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span>
  <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">http</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">request</span>(<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">req</span>)
}
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">puts</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">res</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">body</span>
</pre><h3 id="class-Net::HTTP-label-Streaming+Response+Bodies" style="margin-bottom: 1.2em; font-size: 1.25em; line-height: 1.2; font-family: Georgia, 'Times New Roman', serif; color: rgb(108, 108, 108);">Streaming Response Bodies<span style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#class-Net::HTTP-label-Streaming+Response+Bodies" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">¶</a>&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#top" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">↑&lt;/a></span></h3><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;">By default&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP</a>&nbsp;reads an entire response into memory. If you are handling large files or wish to implement a progress bar you can instead stream the body directly to an IO.</p><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(48, 48, 48);"><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">URI</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'http://example.com/large_file'</span>)

<span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTP</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">start</span>(<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">host</span>, <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">port</span>) <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">do</span> <span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">http</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span>
  <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">request</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTP</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Get</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">new</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span>

  <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">http</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">request</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">request</span> <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">do</span> <span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">response</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span>
    <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">open</span> <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'large_file'</span>, <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'w'</span> <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">do</span> <span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">io</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span>
      <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">response</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">read_body</span> <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">do</span> <span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">chunk</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span>
        <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">io</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">write</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">chunk</span>
      <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">end</span>
    <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">end</span>
  <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">end</span>
<span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">end</span>
</pre><h3 id="class-Net::HTTP-label-HTTPS" style="margin-bottom: 1.2em; font-size: 1.25em; line-height: 1.2; font-family: Georgia, 'Times New Roman', serif; color: rgb(108, 108, 108);">HTTPS<span style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#class-Net::HTTP-label-HTTPS" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">¶</a>&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#top" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">↑&lt;/a></span></h3><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;">HTTPS is enabled for an&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTP</a>&nbsp;connection by&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#method-i-use_ssl-3D" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">#use_ssl=</a>.</p><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(48, 48, 48);"><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">URI</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'https://secure.example.com/some_path?query=string'</span>)
