<span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTP</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">start</span>(<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">host</span>, <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">port</span>,
  :<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">use_ssl</span> =<span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">&gt;</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">scheme</span> <span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">==</span> <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'https'</span>) <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">do</span> <span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">http</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span>
  <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">request</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTP</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Get</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">new</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">uri</span>

  <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">response</span> = <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">http</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">request</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">request</span> <span class="ruby-comment" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(94, 255, 31); font-weight: bold; background: transparent;"># Net::HTTPResponse object</span>
<span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">end</span>
</pre><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;">In previous versions of Ruby you would need to require ‘net/https’ to use HTTPS. This is no longer true.</p><h3 id="class-Net::HTTP-label-Proxies" style="margin-bottom: 1.2em; font-size: 1.25em; line-height: 1.2; font-family: Georgia, 'Times New Roman', serif; color: rgb(108, 108, 108);">Proxies<span style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#class-Net::HTTP-label-Proxies" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">¶</a>&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#top" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">↑&lt;/a></span></h3><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP</a>&nbsp;will automatically create a proxy from the&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">http_proxy</code>&nbsp;environment variable if it is present. To disable use of&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">http_proxy</code>, pass&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">nil</code>&nbsp;for the proxy address.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;">You may also create a custom proxy:</p><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(48, 48, 48);"><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">proxy_addr</span> = <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'your.proxy.host'</span>
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">proxy_port</span> = <span class="ruby-value" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">8080</span>

<span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTP</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">new</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'example.com'</span>, <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">nil</span>, <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">proxy_addr</span>, <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">proxy_port</span>).<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">start</span> { <span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">http</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span>
  <span class="ruby-comment" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(94, 255, 31); font-weight: bold; background: transparent;"># always proxy via your.proxy.addr:8080</span>
}
</pre><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;">See&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#method-c-new" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">::new</a>&nbsp;for further details and examples such as proxies that require a username and password.</p><h3 id="class-Net::HTTP-label-Compression" style="margin-bottom: 1.2em; font-size: 1.25em; line-height: 1.2; font-family: Georgia, 'Times New Roman', serif; color: rgb(108, 108, 108);">Compression<span style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#class-Net::HTTP-label-Compression" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">¶</a>&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#top" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">↑&lt;/a></span></h3><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP</a>&nbsp;automatically adds Accept-Encoding for compression of response bodies and automatically decompresses gzip and deflate responses unless a Range header was sent.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;">Compression can be disabled through the Accept-Encoding: identity header.</p><h2 id="class-Net::HTTP-label-HTTP+Request+Classes" style="margin-bottom: 1em; font-size: 1.5em; line-height: 1; font-family: Georgia, 'Times New Roman', serif; color: rgb(108, 108, 108);"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: none; color: rgb(204, 51, 51);">HTTP</a>&nbsp;Request Classes<span style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#class-Net::HTTP-label-HTTP+Request+Classes" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: none; color: rgb(204, 51, 51);">¶</a>&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#top" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: none; color: rgb(204, 51, 51);">↑&lt;/a></span></h2><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;">Here is the&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTP</a>&nbsp;request class hierarchy.</p><ul style="padding: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em; margin-left: 1.5em;"><li style="line-height: 1.4em;"><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTPRequest.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTPRequest</a></p><ul style="padding: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-left: 1.5em;"><li style="line-height: 1.4em;"><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP/Get.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP::Get</a></p></li><li style="line-height: 1.4em;"><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP/Head.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP::Head</a></p></li><li style="line-height: 1.4em;"><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP/Post.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP::Post</a></p></li><li style="line-height: 1.4em;"><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP/Patch.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP::Patch</a></p></li><li style="line-height: 1.4em;"><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP/Put.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP::Put</a></p></li><li style="line-height: 1.4em;"><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP/Proppatch.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: none; color: rgb(204, 51, 51);">↑&lt;/a></span></h2><p style="padding: 0px; margin: 1em 0.4em;">Here is&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; All classes are defined in&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); margin: 1em 0.4em;">There is also the Net::HTTPBadResponse exception which is raised when there is a protocol error.</p></div><div id="5Buntitled-5D" class="documentation-section" style="font-family: Georgia, 'Times New Roman', serif; margin: 0px; font-size: 10.8px; text-transform: uppercase; vertical-align: super;">[R]</span></div><div class="method-description 245" style="margin: 5px 20px;"><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Seconds to wait for 100 Continue response. If the&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTP</a>&nbsp;object does not receive a response in this many seconds it sends the request body. The default value is&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">nil</code>.</p></div></div><div id="keep_alive_timeout-attribute-method" class="method-detail" style="padding-top: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; cursor: pointer;"><a name="keep_alive_timeout" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><a name="keep_alive_timeout=" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading attribute-method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: url("../images/tag_green.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-name" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">keep_alive_timeout</span><span class="attribute-access-type" style="padding: 0px 2px; margin: 0px; font-size: 10.8px; text-transform: uppercase; vertical-align: super;">[RW]</span></div><div class="method-description 245" style="margin: 5px 20px;"><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Seconds to reuse the connection of the previous request. If the idle time is less than this Keep-Alive Timeout,&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP</a>&nbsp;reuses the TCP/IP socket used by the previous communication. The default value is 2 seconds.</p></div></div><div id="key-attribute-method" class="method-detail" style="padding-top: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; cursor: pointer;"><a name="key" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><a name="key=" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading attribute-method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: url("../images/tag_green.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-name" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">key</span><span class="attribute-access-type" style="padding: 0px 2px; margin: 0px; font-size: 10.8px; text-transform: uppercase; vertical-align: super;">[RW]</span></div><div class="method-description 245" style="margin: 5px 20px;"><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Sets an OpenSSL::PKey::RSA or OpenSSL::PKey::DSA object. (This method is appeared in Michal Rokos’s OpenSSL extension.)</p></div></div><div id="local_host-attribute-method" class="method-detail" style="padding-top: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; background-color: rgb(222, 222, 222);">Public Class Methods</h3><div id="Proxy-method" class="method-detail " style="padding-top: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; margin: 0px;">Proxy</span><span class="method-args" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">(p_addr = :ENV, p_port = nil, p_user = nil, p_pass = nil)</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Creates an&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTP</a>&nbsp;proxy class which behaves like&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP</a>, but performs all access via the specified proxy.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">This class is obsolete. You may pass these same parameters directly to&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#method-c-new" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">::new</a>. See&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#method-c-new" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">::new</a>for details of the arguments.</p></div></div><div id="default_port-method" class="method-detail " style="padding-top: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; cursor: pointer;"><a name="method-c-default_port" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: url("../images/brick.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-name" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">default_port</span><span class="method-args" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">()</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">The default port to use for&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTP</a>&nbsp;requests; defaults to 80.</p></div></div><div id="get-method" class="method-detail " style="padding-top: 0.5em; border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: url("../images/brick.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-name" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">get</span><span class="method-args" style="padding: 0px; visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Sends a GET request to the target and returns the&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTP</a>&nbsp;response as a string. The target can either be specified as (<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">uri</code>), or as (<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">host</code>,&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">path</code>,&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">port</code>&nbsp;= 80); so:</p><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(48, 48, 48);"><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">print</span> <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTP</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">get</span>(<span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">URI</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'http://www.example.com/index.html'</span>))
</pre><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">or:</p><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(48, 48, 48);"><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">print</span> <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTP</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">get</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'www.example.com'</span>, <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'/index.html'</span>)
</pre></div></div><div id="get_print-method" class="method-detail " style="padding-top: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; cursor: pointer;"><a name="method-c-get_print" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: url("../images/brick.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-name" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">get_print</span><span class="method-args" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">(uri_or_host, path = nil, port = nil)</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Gets the body text from the target and outputs it to $stdout. The target can either be specified as (<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">uri</code>), or as (<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">host</code>,&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">path</code>,&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">port</code>&nbsp;= 80); so:</p><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(48, 48, 48);"><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTP</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">get_print</span> <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">URI</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'http://www.example.com/index.html'</span>)

</pre></div></div><div id="get_response-method" class="method-detail " style="padding-top: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; cursor: pointer;"><a name="method-c-get_response" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: url("../images/brick.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-name" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">get_response</span><span class="method-args" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">(uri_or_host, path = nil, port = nil, &amp;block)</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Sends a GET request to the target and returns the&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTP</a>&nbsp;response as a<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTPResponse.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTPResponse</a>&nbsp;object. The target can either be specified as (<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">uri</code>), or as (<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">host</code>,&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">path</code>,<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">port</code>&nbsp;= 80); so:</p><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(48, 48, 48);"><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">res</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTP</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">get_response</span>(<span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">URI</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'http://www.example.com/index.html'</span>))
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">print</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">res</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">body</span>
</pre><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">or:</p><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(48, 48, 48);"><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">res</span> = <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTP</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">get_response</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'www.example.com'</span>, <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'/index.html'</span>)
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">print</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">res</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">body</span>
</pre></div></div><div id="http_default_port-method" class="method-detail " style="padding-top: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; cursor: pointer;"><a name="method-c-http_default_port" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: url("../images/brick.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-name" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">http_default_port</span><span class="method-args" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">()</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">The default port to use for&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTP</a>&nbsp;requests; defaults to 80.</p></div></div><div id="https_default_port-method" class="method-detail " style="padding-top: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; cursor: pointer;"><a name="method-c-https_default_port" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: url("../images/brick.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-name" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">https_default_port</span><span class="method-args" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">()</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">The default port to use for HTTPS requests; defaults to 443.</p></div></div><div id="is_version_1_2-3F-method" class="method-detail method-alias" style="padding-top: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; cursor: pointer;"><a name="method-c-is_version_1_2-3F" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(0, 102, 136); background: url("../images/brick_link.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-name" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">is_version_1_2?</span><span class="method-args" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">()</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div></div><div class="aliases" style="padding-top: 4px; margin: 5px 20px; font-style: italic; cursor: default;">Alias for:&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#method-c-version_1_2-3F" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">version_1_2?</a></div></div><div id="new-method" class="method-detail " style="padding-top: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; cursor: pointer;"><a name="method-c-new" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: url("../images/brick.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-name" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">new</span><span class="method-args" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">(address, port = nil, p_addr = :ENV, p_port = nil, p_user = nil, p_pass = nil)</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Creates a new&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP</a>&nbsp;object without opening a TCP connection or&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTP</a>&nbsp;session.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">The&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">address</code>&nbsp;should be a DNS hostname or IP address, the&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">port</code>&nbsp;is the port the server operates on. If no&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">port</code>&nbsp;is given the default port for&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTP</a>&nbsp;or HTTPS is used.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">If none of the&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">p_</code>&nbsp;arguments are given, the proxy host and port are taken from the<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">http_proxy</code>&nbsp;environment variable (or its uppercase equivalent) if present. If the proxy requires authentication you must supply it by hand. See URI::Generic#find_proxy for details of proxy detection from the environment. To disable proxy detection set&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">p_addr</code>&nbsp;to nil.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">If you are connecting to a custom proxy,&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">p_addr</code>&nbsp;the DNS name or IP address of the proxy host,&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">p_port</code>&nbsp;the port to use to access the proxy, and&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">p_user</code>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">p_pass</code>&nbsp;the username and password if authorization is required to use the proxy.</p></div><div class="aliases" style="padding-top: 4px; margin: 5px 20px; font-style: italic; cursor: default;">Also aliased as:&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#method-c-newobj" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">newobj</a></div></div><div id="new-method" class="method-detail " style="padding-top: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; cursor: pointer;"><a name="method-c-new" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: url("../images/brick.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-name" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">new</span><span class="method-args" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">(address, port = nil)</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Creates a new&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP</a>&nbsp;object for the specified server address, without opening the TCP connection or initializing the&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTP</a>&nbsp;session. The&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">address</code>&nbsp;should be a DNS hostname or IP address.</p></div></div><div id="newobj-method" class="method-detail method-alias" style="padding-top: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; cursor: pointer;"><a name="method-c-newobj" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(0, 102, 136); background: url("../images/brick_link.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-name" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">newobj</span><span class="method-args" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">(address, port = nil, p_addr = :ENV, p_port = nil, p_user = nil, p_pass = nil)</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div></div><div class="aliases" style="padding-top: 4px; margin: 5px 20px; font-style: italic; cursor: default;">Alias for:&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#method-c-new" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">new</a></div></div><div id="post_form-method" class="method-detail " style="padding-top: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; cursor: pointer;"><a name="method-c-post_form" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: url("../images/brick.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-name" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">post_form</span><span class="method-args" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">(url, params)</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Posts HTML form data to the specified URI object. The form data must be provided as a Hash mapping from String to String. Example:</p><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(48, 48, 48);">{ <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">"cmd"</span> =<span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">&gt;</span> <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">"search"</span>, <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">"q"</span> =<span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">&gt;</span> <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">"ruby"</span>, <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">"max"</span> =<span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">&gt;</span> <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">"50"</span> }
</pre><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">This method also does Basic Authentication iff&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">url</code>.user exists. But userinfo for authentication is deprecated (RFC3986). So this feature will be removed.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Example:</p><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(48, 48, 48);"><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">require</span> <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'net/http'</span>
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">require</span> <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'uri'</span>

<span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTP</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">post_form</span> <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">URI</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'http://www.example.com/search.cgi'</span>),
                    { <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">"q"</span> =<span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">&gt;</span> <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">"ruby"</span>, <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">"max"</span> =<span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">&gt;</span> <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">"50"</span> }
</pre></div></div><div id="proxy_class-3F-method" class="method-detail " style="padding-top: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; cursor: pointer;"><a name="method-c-proxy_class-3F" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: url("../images/brick.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-name" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">proxy_class?</span><span class="method-args" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">()</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">returns true if self is a class which was created by HTTP::Proxy.</p></div></div><div id="start-method" class="method-detail " style="padding-top: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; cursor: pointer;"><a name="method-c-start" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: url("../images/brick.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-callseq" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">start(address, port, p_addr, p_port, p_user, p_pass, &amp;block)</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: url("../images/brick.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-callseq" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">start(address, port=nil, p_addr=nil, p_port=nil, p_user=nil, p_pass=nil, opt, &amp;block)</span></div><div><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Creates a new&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP</a>&nbsp;object, then additionally opens the TCP connection and&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTP</a>session.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Arguments are the following:</p><dl class="rdoc-list note-list" style="padding: 0px; margin: 8px 1.5em; border: 1px solid rgb(204, 204, 204);"><dt style="padding: 2px 4px; margin: 0px; background: rgb(221, 221, 221);"><em style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-weight: inherit;">address</em></dt><dd style="padding: 2px 12px; margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">hostname or IP address of the server</p></dd><dt style="padding: 2px 4px; margin: 0.7em 0px 0px; background: rgb(221, 221, 221);"><em style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-weight: inherit;">port</em></dt><dd style="padding: 2px 12px; margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">port of the server</p></dd><dt style="padding: 2px 4px; margin: 0.7em 0px 0px; background: rgb(221, 221, 221);"><em style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-weight: inherit;">p_addr</em></dt><dd style="padding: 2px 12px; margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">address of proxy</p></dd><dt style="padding: 2px 4px; margin: 0.7em 0px 0px; background: rgb(221, 221, 221);"><em style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-weight: inherit;">p_port</em></dt><dd style="padding: 2px 12px; margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">port of proxy</p></dd><dt style="padding: 2px 4px; margin: 0.7em 0px 0px; background: rgb(221, 221, 221);"><em style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-weight: inherit;">p_user</em></dt><dd style="padding: 2px 12px; margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">user of proxy</p></dd><dt style="padding: 2px 4px; margin: 0.7em 0px 0px; background: rgb(221, 221, 221);"><em style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-weight: inherit;">p_pass</em></dt><dd style="padding: 2px 12px; margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">pass of proxy</p></dd><dt style="padding: 2px 4px; margin: 0.7em 0px 0px; background: rgb(221, 221, 221);"><em style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-weight: inherit;">opt</em></dt><dd style="padding: 2px 12px; margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">optional hash</p></dd></dl><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;"><em style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-weight: inherit;">opt</em>&nbsp;sets following values by its accessor. The keys are&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#attribute-i-ca_file" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">#ca_file</a>,&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#attribute-i-ca_path" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">#ca_path</a>, cert,<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#attribute-i-cert_store" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">#cert_store</a>, ciphers,&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#attribute-i-close_on_empty_response" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">#close_on_empty_response</a>, key,&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#attribute-i-open_timeout" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">#open_timeout</a>,<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#attribute-i-read_timeout" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">#read_timeout</a>,&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#attribute-i-ssl_timeout" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">#ssl_timeout</a>,&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#attribute-i-ssl_version" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">#ssl_version</a>, use_ssl,&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#attribute-i-verify_callback" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">#verify_callback</a>,&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#attribute-i-verify_depth" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">#verify_depth</a>and verify_mode. If you set :use_ssl as true, you can use https and default value of<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#attribute-i-verify_mode" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">#verify_mode</a>&nbsp;is set as OpenSSL::SSL::VERIFY_PEER.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">If the optional block is given, the newly created&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP</a>&nbsp;object is passed to it and closed when the block finishes. In this case, the return value of this method is the return value of the block. If no block is given, the return value of this method is the newly created&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP</a>&nbsp;object itself, and the caller is responsible for closing it upon completion using the finish() method.</p></div></div><div id="version_1_2-method" class="method-detail " style="padding-top: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; cursor: pointer;"><a name="method-c-version_1_2" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: url("../images/brick.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-name" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">version_1_2</span><span class="method-args" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">()</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Turns on net/http 1.2 (Ruby 1.8) features. Defaults to ON in Ruby 1.8 or later.</p></div></div><div id="version_1_2-3F-method" class="method-detail " style="padding-top: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; cursor: pointer;"><a name="method-c-version_1_2-3F" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: url("../images/brick.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-name" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">version_1_2?</span><span class="method-args" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">()</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Returns true if net/http is in version 1.2 mode. Defaults to true.</p></div><div class="aliases" style="padding-top: 4px; margin: 5px 20px; font-style: italic; cursor: default;">Also aliased as:&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#method-c-is_version_1_2-3F" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">is_version_1_2?</a></div></div></div><div id="public-instance-method-details" class="method-section section" style="font-size: 14.4px;"><h3 class="section-header" style="padding: 0.75em 0.5em; margin-top: 2em; margin-bottom: 1.2em; font-size: 21.6px; line-height: 1.2; font-family: Georgia, 'Times New Roman', serif; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); border: 1px solid rgb(187, 187, 187); border-radius: 3px; background-color: rgb(222, 222, 222);">Public Instance Methods</h3><div id="active-3F-method" class="method-detail method-alias" style="padding-top: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: url("../images/brick.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-name" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">copy</span><span class="method-args" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">(path, initheader = nil)</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Sends a COPY request to the&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">path</code>&nbsp;and gets a response, as an&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTPResponse.html" style="padding: 0px; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; cursor: pointer;"><a name="method-i-delete" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: url("../images/brick.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-name" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">delete</span><span class="method-args" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">(path, initheader = {'Depth' =&gt; 'Infinity'})</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Sends a DELETE request to the&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">path</code>&nbsp;and gets a response, as an&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTPResponse.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTPResponse</a>&nbsp;object.</p></div></div><div id="finish-method" class="method-detail " style="padding-top: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; cursor: pointer;"><a name="method-i-finish" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: url("../images/brick.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-name" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">finish</span><span class="method-args" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">()</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Finishes the&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTP</a>&nbsp;session and closes the TCP connection. Raises IOError if the session has not been started.</p></div></div><div id="get-method" class="method-detail " style="padding-top: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; cursor: pointer;"><a name="method-i-get" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: url("../images/brick.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-name" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">get</span><span class="method-args" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">(path, initheader = nil, dest = nil)</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Retrieves data from&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">path</code>&nbsp;on the connected-to host which may be an absolute path String or a URI to extract the path from.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;"><code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">initheader</code>&nbsp;must be a Hash like { 'Accept' =&gt; '<strong style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-style: inherit;">/</strong>', ... }, and it defaults to an empty hash. If<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">initheader</code>&nbsp;doesn't have the key 'accept-encoding', then a value of "gzip;q=1.0,deflate;q=0.6,identity;q=0.3" is used, so that gzip compression is used in preference to deflate compression, which is used in preference to no compression. Ruby doesn't have libraries to support the compress (Lempel-Ziv) compression, so that is not supported. The intent of this is to reduce bandwidth by default. If this routine sets up compression, then it does the decompression also, removing the header as well to prevent confusion. Otherwise it leaves the body as it found it.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">This method returns a&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTPResponse.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTPResponse</a>&nbsp;object.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">If called with a block, yields each fragment of the entity body in turn as a string as it is read from the socket. Note that in this case, the returned response object will&nbsp;<strong style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-style: inherit;">not</strong>contain a (meaningful) body.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;"><code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">dest</code>&nbsp;argument is obsolete. It still works but you must not use it.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">This method never raises an exception.</p><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(48, 48, 48);"><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">response</span> = <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">http</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">get</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'/index.html'</span>)

<span class="ruby-comment" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(94, 255, 31); font-weight: bold; background: transparent;"># using block</span>
<span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">File</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">open</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'result.txt'</span>, <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'w'</span>) {<span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">f</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span>
  <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">http</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">get</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'/~foo/'</span>) <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">do</span> <span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">str</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span>
    <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">f</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">write</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">str</span>
  <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">end</span>
}
</pre></div></div><div id="get2-method" class="method-detail method-alias" style="padding-top: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; cursor: pointer;"><a name="method-i-get2" style="padding: 0px; border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: url("../images/brick.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-name" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">head</span><span class="method-args" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">(path, initheader = nil)</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Gets only the header from&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; ‘&lt;strong style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-style: inherit;">/</strong>’, … }.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">This method returns a&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTPResponse.html" style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">This method never raises an exception.</p><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; <span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">Net</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">::</span><span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">HTTP</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">start</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'some.www.server'</span>, <span class="ruby-value" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">80</span>) {<span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">http</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span>
  <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">response</span> = <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">http</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">head</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'/index.html'</span>)

border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">path</code>&nbsp;and gets a response, as an&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTPResponse.html" style="padding: 0px; border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; margin: 0px;">()</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden;
