padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; cursor: pointer;"><a name="method-i-post" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: url("../images/brick.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-name" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">post</span><span class="method-args" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">(path, data, initheader = nil, dest = nil)</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Posts&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">data</code>&nbsp;(must be a String) to&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">path</code>.&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">header</code>&nbsp;must be a Hash like { ‘Accept’ =&gt; ‘&lt;strong style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-style: inherit;">/</strong>’, … }.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">This method returns a&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTPResponse.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTPResponse</a>&nbsp;object.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">If called with a block, yields each fragment of the entity body in turn as a string as it is read from the socket. Note that in this case, the returned response object will&nbsp;<strong style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-style: inherit;">not</strong>contain a (meaningful) body.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;"><code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">dest</code>&nbsp;argument is obsolete. It still works but you must not use it.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">This method never raises exception.</p><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(48, 48, 48);"><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">response</span> = <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">http</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">post</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'/cgi-bin/search.rb'</span>, <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'query=foo'</span>)

<span class="ruby-comment" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(94, 255, 31); font-weight: bold; background: transparent;"># using block</span>
<span class="ruby-constant" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(127, 255, 212); background: transparent;">File</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">open</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'result.txt'</span>, <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'w'</span>) {<span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">f</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span>
  <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">http</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">post</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'/cgi-bin/search.rb'</span>, <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'query=foo'</span>) <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">do</span> <span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">str</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span>
    <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">f</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">write</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">str</span>
  <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">end</span>
}
</pre><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">You should set Content-Type: header field for POST. If no Content-Type: field given, this method uses “application/x-www-form-urlencoded” by default.</p></div></div><div id="post2-method" class="method-detail method-alias" style="padding-top: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; cursor: pointer;"><a name="method-i-read_timeout-3D" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; cursor: pointer;"><a name="method-i-request" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: url("../images/brick.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-name" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">request</span><span class="method-args" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">(req, body = nil)</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Sends an&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTPRequest.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTPRequest</a>&nbsp;object&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">req</code>&nbsp;to the&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTP</a>&nbsp;server.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">If&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">req</code>&nbsp;is a&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP/Post.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP::Post</a>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP/Put.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP::Put</a>&nbsp;request containing data, the data is also sent. Providing data for a&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP/Head.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP::Head</a>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP/Get.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP::Get</a>&nbsp;request results in an ArgumentError.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Returns an&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTPResponse.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTPResponse</a>&nbsp;object.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">When called with a block, passes an&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTPResponse.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTPResponse</a>&nbsp;object to the block. The body of the response will not have been read yet; the block can process it using<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTPResponse.html#method-i-read_body" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTPResponse#read_body</a>, if desired.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">This method never raises Net::* exceptions.</p></div></div><div id="request_get-method" class="method-detail " style="padding-top: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; cursor: pointer;"><a name="method-i-request_get" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: url("../images/brick.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-name" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">request_get</span><span class="method-args" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">(path, initheader = nil)</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Sends a GET request to the&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">path</code>. Returns the response as a&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTPResponse.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTPResponse</a>&nbsp;object.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">When called with a block, passes an&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTPResponse.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTPResponse</a>&nbsp;object to the block. The body of the response will not have been read yet; the block can process it using<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTPResponse.html#method-i-read_body" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTPResponse#read_body</a>, if desired.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Returns the response.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">This method never raises Net::* exceptions.</p><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(48, 48, 48);"><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">response</span> = <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">http</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">request_get</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'/index.html'</span>)
<span class="ruby-comment" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(94, 255, 31); font-weight: bold; background: transparent;"># The entity body is already read in this case.</span>
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">p</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">response</span>[<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'content-type'</span>]
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">puts</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">response</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">body</span>

<span class="ruby-comment" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(94, 255, 31); font-weight: bold; background: transparent;"># Using a block</span>
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">http</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">request_get</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'/index.html'</span>) {<span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">response</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span>
  <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">p</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">response</span>[<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'content-type'</span>]
  <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">response</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">read_body</span> <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">do</span> <span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">str</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span>   <span class="ruby-comment" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(94, 255, 31); font-weight: bold; background: transparent;"># read body now</span>
    <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">print</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">str</span>
  <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">end</span>
}

margin: 0px;">(path, data, initheader = nil)</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Sends a POST request to the&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">path</code>.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Returns the response as a&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTPResponse.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTPResponse</a>&nbsp;object.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">When called with a block, the block is passed an&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTPResponse.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTPResponse</a>&nbsp;object. The body of that response will not have been read yet; the block can process it using<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTPResponse.html#method-i-read_body" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTPResponse#read_body</a>, if desired.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Returns the response.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">This method never raises Net::* exceptions.</p><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(48, 48, 48);"><span class="ruby-comment" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(94, 255, 31); font-weight: bold; background: transparent;"># example</span>
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">response</span> = <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">http</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">request_post</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'/cgi-bin/nice.rb'</span>, <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'datadatadata...'</span>)
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">p</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">response</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">status</span>
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">puts</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">response</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">body</span>          <span class="ruby-comment" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(94, 255, 31); font-weight: bold; background: transparent;"># body is already read in this case</span>

<span class="ruby-comment" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(94, 255, 31); font-weight: bold; background: transparent;"># using block</span>
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">http</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">request_post</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'/cgi-bin/nice.rb'</span>, <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'datadatadata...'</span>) {<span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">response</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span>
  <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">p</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">response</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">status</span>
  <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">p</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">response</span>[<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'content-type'</span>]
  <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">response</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">read_body</span> <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">do</span> <span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">str</span><span class="ruby-operator" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 238); background: transparent;">|</span>   <span class="ruby-comment" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(94, 255, 31); font-weight: bold; background: transparent;"># read body now</span>
    <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">print</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">str</span>
  <span class="ruby-keyword" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 255, 255); background: transparent;">end</span>
}
</pre></div><div class="aliases" style="padding-top: 4px; margin: 5px 20px; font-style: italic; cursor: default;">Also aliased as:&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html#method-i-post2" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">post2</a></div></div><div id="send_request-method" class="method-detail " style="padding-top: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; cursor: pointer;"><a name="method-i-send_request" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: url("../images/brick.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-name" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">send_request</span><span class="method-args" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">(name, path, data = nil, header = nil)</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Sends an&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTP</a>&nbsp;request to the&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTP</a>&nbsp;server. Also sends a DATA string if&nbsp;<code style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">data</code>&nbsp;is given.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Returns a&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTPResponse.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTPResponse</a>&nbsp;object.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">This method never raises Net::* exceptions.</p><pre class="ruby" style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background: rgb(48, 48, 48);"><span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">response</span> = <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">http</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">send_request</span>(<span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'GET'</span>, <span class="ruby-string" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">'/index.html'</span>)
<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">puts</span> <span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">response</span>.<span class="ruby-identifier" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 222, 173); background: transparent;">body</span>
</pre></div></div><div id="set_debug_output-method" class="method-detail " style="padding-top: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; cursor: pointer;"><a name="method-i-set_debug_output" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: url("../images/brick.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-name" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">set_debug_output</span><span class="method-args" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">(output)</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;"><strong style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; font-style: inherit;">WARNING</strong>&nbsp;This method opens a serious security hole. Never use this method in production code.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Sets an output stream for debugging.</p><pre style="padding: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 24px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background: rgb(221, 221, 221);">http = Net::HTTP.new(hostname)
http.set_debug_output $stderr
http.start { .... }</pre></div></div><div id="start-method" class="method-detail " style="padding-top: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; cursor: pointer;"><a name="method-i-start" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: url("../images/brick.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-name" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">start</span><span class="method-args" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">()</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Opens a TCP connection and&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTP</a>&nbsp;session.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">When this method is called with a block, it passes the&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">Net::HTTP</a>&nbsp;object to the block, and closes the TCP connection and&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTP</a>&nbsp;session after the block has been executed.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">When called with a block, it returns the return value of the block; otherwise, it returns self.</p></div></div><div id="started-3F-method" class="method-detail " style="padding-top: 0.5em; padding-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em; cursor: pointer;"><a name="method-i-started-3F" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: url("../images/brick.png") 0% 100% no-repeat;"><span class="method-name" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">started?</span><span class="method-args" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px;">()</span><span class="method-click-advice" style="padding: 0px 20px 0px 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 2px; right: 5px; font-size: 10px; color: rgb(155, 152, 119); visibility: hidden; line-height: 20px; background: url("../images/zoom.png") 100% 0% no-repeat;"></span></div><div><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Returns true if the&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">HTTP</a>&nbsp;session has been started.</p></div><div class="aliases" style="padding-top: 4px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;">active?</a></div></div><div id="trace-method" class="method-detail " style="padding-top: 0.5em; margin: 0px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1;">path</code>&nbsp;and gets a response, as an&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTPResponse.html" style="padding: 0px; border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important;"></a><div class="method-heading" style="padding-top: 2px; padding-right: 4px; padding-left: 20px; position: relative; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; This flag must be set before starting session. If you change use_ssl value after session started, a&nbsp;<a href="http://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.3.1/libdoc/net/http/rdoc/Net/HTTP.html" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">Commenting is here to help enhance the documentation. For example, code samples, or clarification of the documentation.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">If you have questions about Ruby or the documentation, please post to one of the&nbsp;<a href="http://www.ruby-lang.org/en/community/mailing-lists/" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important; font-weight: bold !important;">Ruby mailing lists</a>. You will get better, faster, help that way.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">If you wish to post a correction of the docs, please do so, but also&nbsp;<a href="http://bugs.ruby-lang.org/" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important; font-weight: bold !important;">file bug report</a>&nbsp;so that it can be corrected for the next release. Thank you.</p><p style="padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 1.5em;">If you want to help improve the Ruby documentation, please visit<a href="http://documenting-ruby.org/" style="padding: 0px; margin: 0px; opacity: 1; border-bottom-style: dotted; border-bottom-color: rgb(205, 205, 205); border-bottom-width: 1px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51) !important; font-weight: bold !important;">Documenting-ruby.org</a>.</p></div><div id="5Buntitled-5D" class="documentation-section"><div id="public-instance-method-details" class="method-section section"><div id="proxy_user-method" class="method-detail ">
